## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="1323c-963">Атрибуты Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1323c-963">Windows Server 2003 R2 Attributes</span></span>
